< rating>
5</rating>
<Text>This park represents my youth. In the day time, children play here and you can lay down in the grass or play Frisbee. At night, the lights of the basketball court and tennis are left on. The tennis courts are usually empty at night, but in the basketball courts are filled with young men and boys shooting hoops together. I love sitting here at the picnic tables with my SO and hearing the sounds the ball makes on the pavement, the sounds of their banter. When I was younger, my teenage friends and I would spend the night on the play structures watching the stars. The area is safe - patrols come by to check on everyone all night, but they manage to do it discretely and respectfully, which I love. Bless this park <3< /Text><Pictures>None< /Pictures>< Resp>

I got off work around 5:30 this evening and was desperate to find an open florist (grumpy girlfriend at home!).  I called here and got a hold of Ashley who was trying to close down for the night.  She offered to wait for me to arrive saying she'd be happy to show me some of their pre-arranged bouquets before she locked up.

<rate>4<//rate><Text>I'd like to start out saying that we just got home from the best trip of our lives! We spent about 10 days traveling as a family of 6 through CA, AZ, UT & NV. Absolutely the greatest thing we've ever done! We have 4 kids (10, 10, 8, 3) and we rented the largest RV Cruise America has available.

Pros:
It fit us comfortably and was a great size for this length trip. Beds were comfortable. Cab bed is actually bigger than a Queen (our queen sheets did not fit, which was a bummer, but great to have such a big bed) and our 3 older kids all fit on It to sleep. I was happily surprised by all the storage space throughout! Cupboards were big enough for large bins with kids things and baskets of food. Kitchen storage was good-fit a decent amount of kitchenware and pantry items. The bathroom also had a great amount of storage (medicine cabinet, storage below sink, two cupboards up above toilet and several little shelves next to sink). Queen bed in back was comfortable and the cupboards were large.

Generator was super helpful when driving through hot desert days and the cost was totally worth it.

Nice simple, modern design.

Cons:
The moment I opened the refrigerator, the trailer smelled terribly. At first, I thought it was from food previously in the fridge. But upon further thought, I believe it's an air filtration issue with the rig. It's a big problem-it smells very badly and each time we opened the door (which is a lot) we'd have to spray something to make the air smell nice. (Even my 3 year old yelled GROSS every time we opened the fridge).) After noticing the smell of the fridge, we noticed that a lot of the vehicle wasn't cleaned great. My wife bleached down every surface (including fridge) and the wipes were dark brown by the end. That was a little disappointing for the price you pay to rent these, especially in this season of Covid. We expected to receive a clean RV.

This trailer is LOUD. Bumpy and very, very, loud. Don't expect to listen to much music or hear each other talk. We had to basically yell if we wanted to hear one another. By the end of the first day my wife could tell something was off-she kept hearing wind inside the vehicle. She found part of the wall of the trailer was separating from the cab of the truck. While I was driving, she could see light coming through the side wall and could see a 1/4" of the road through the floor! She was terrified and was genuinely worried that the trailer was coming apart. I had to fix it two separate times on the trip. On the outside where the cab connects to the trailer, there should be about 12 screws. We had 3. Not sure how that got overlooked? Seems like a pretty big error.

We are already talking about planning another trip, but not sure we'd use a rig like this again with how loud it was? We'd like to "enjoy" the journey a bit more without the clanking and sounds of wind... maybe it was just our trailer? But it's not cheap and not sure we'd want to chance it again.

All in all, again, it was the greatest family trip we've ever had! We are so thankful for this experience!< /Text>< pics>

<Text>Be prepared to deal with dishonest people.

We rented an RV for 3 days: 6/16 through 6/19. We left it in the driveway on 6/18 and put the key in the drop-off box. Nevertheless, we were charged $25 for being one hour late. I spoke to Jackie over the phone. She told me that the record shows that the RV was returned at 12:20pm on 6/19, i.e. after the deadline of 11am. She refused to refund us $25 even when I told her that the record was wrong and the RV was returned on 6/18, not on 6/19.

They also charged us $50 for cleaning. I told Jackie that the RV was clean when we returned it, and it was in the same condition when we had picked it up. I asked her to provide us with photos showing that it was not clean. She said she had no photos and again refused to refund $50. "We charged $50, so it must have been dirty," she explained. "Well, you charged us $25 for late fees even though we were not late," I responded. No reaction.

<review>I usually don't review health providers, but this dental office was too unique not to talk about.

I needed cleaning and filling, and as every time I go to a dentist, I was nervous about the pain.

From the minute I entered the place, I felt it was quite different from other offices I have been to. It feels like you are in a high end spa... Very nice decor, colors and feel. They even have birds and nature sounds in the background, and their chairs have massage features... It really feels relaxing!

I was impressed with the doctor's bedside manners. Very good listener, and patient in explaining what went wrong with my teeth and the treatment he would use for that. He even pointed out my most economical options (very rare to find in a dentist!!). Don't be shy to ask if they can give you a payment plan.

During the procedure, the doctor paused from time to time to ask me how I was feeling and encouraged me to tell him if I had any concern or feel any pain. I really like that personal care and attention, versus feeling I'm on a conveyor belt, and rushed out the door (I'm sure a lot of people can relate to that lol ).
